"Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes." "Raw fastq files from sequencing runs were processed as follows: Atropos was used to remove the adapter sequences from all the reads; STAR aligner was used to map the reads to the human hg38 genome; RSEM was used to quantitate the reads for each individual gene. Finally, the TPM values were used to represent the mRNA expression of each individual genes."
